However, what truly constitutes Locked Throat Wind is exceedingly strange and urgent, and little is known about it.

While in Yandu, I once encountered a girl who had reached the age of maturity. One day in mid-autumn, she suddenly developed a tight and constricted throat without any preceding illness, and her breathing became labored. Within half a day, her condition worsened significantly. When I was called to treat her, I examined her pulse and found no sign of heat. When I asked about her throat, there was neither swelling nor pain. Observing her appearance, her face was pale and her eyes wide, unable to speak. Listening to her voice, it was as delicate as a needle, and her attempts to breathe were desperate like a thread; she strained her neck as if fighting for her life, in a state of pitiable distress. I was left in doubt, unable to comprehend the situation.[81p]

然意谓风邪闭塞喉窍，非用辛温不能解散，遂以二陈汤加生姜，煎而与之，毫忽无效。意复用独参汤以救其肺，然见其势危若此，恐滋怨谤，终亦未敢下手。他医见之，亦但束手而已。如此者，一日夜而殁。后又一人亦如此而殁。若此二人者，余至今莫识其所以病，此终身之疑窦，殊自愧也。然意必肺气竭绝而然，倘再有值此者，恐非独参汤决不能救。故笔诸此，以俟后之君子虚心详酌焉。　　杨梅结毒，有喉间溃烂作痛，久而不愈者，此非喉痹之属，乃杨梅疮毒也。宜仙遗粮汤；甚者宜以土茯苓煎汤，吞五宝丹。
　　　　石室秘箓 【清　陈士铎】[82p]

The intention is to indicate that the wind pathogen obstructs the throat passages; it cannot be resolved without using pungent and warming herbs. Thus, I added fresh ginger to Erchen Decoction, brewed it, and administered it, but there was no effect at all. I intended to use Dushen Decoction to save the lungs; however, seeing the condition so dire, I feared it would stir grievances and slander, and I ultimately did not dare to take action. Other physicians, upon seeing this, could only stand by without taking any measures. In this way, one person passed away after a day and night. Subsequently, another person met the same fate. As for these two individuals, I still do not understand the cause of their illness, which remains a lifelong perplexity, and I feel deeply ashamed. Nevertheless, it must be that the lung qi was completely exhausted. If another case arises, I fear that Dushen Decoction alone cannot provide salvation. Therefore, I record this here, hoping that future gentlemen will take it to heart and consider it carefully.

Shishis Secret Manuscript 【Qing Dynasty, Chen Shiduo】[82p]

　　　　　肿痛

　　人有喉患大肿，又非瘿瘤，忽痛忽不痛，外现五色之纹，中按之，半空半实，此乃痰病结成，似瘤非瘤，似瘿非瘿也。方用海藻、半夏、白芥子、贝母、人参、桔梗、南星各三钱，茯苓五钱，昆布、甘草各一钱，附子一分，水煎服。此方乃消上焦之痰圣药也。又有海藻、昆布，以去其瘿瘤之外象，消其五色之奇纹。妙在消痰而仍不损气，则胃气健而痰易化也。一剂知，二剂消大半，三剂则全消，四剂永不再发。此方兼可治瘿证，神效。　　凡人有咽喉忽肿作痛，生双蛾者，饮食不能下，五日不食即死矣。但此证实火易治，而虚火难医。实火方，如用山豆根、芩、连、半夏、柴胡、甘草、桔梗、天花粉治之，立消。惟虚火乃肾火不藏于命门，浮游于咽喉之间。其证亦如实火，惟夜重于日，清晨反觉少轻；若实火，清晨反重，夜间反轻。实火，口燥热干而开裂；虚火，口不甚渴舌滑而不裂也。以此辨证，断不差错。[83p]

Swelling and Pain

When a person has a throat condition with significant swelling, which is neither a goiter nor a tumor, the pain may come and go. Externally, there are colorful patterns visible, and when pressed, it feels both empty and solid. This is due to phlegm disease that manifests like a tumor but is neither truly one nor a goiter. The prescription consists of 9 grams each of seaweed, banxia (Pinellia), white mustard seed, fritillaria, ginseng, platycodon (bellflower), and nanking (south stars), 15 grams of poria, 3 grams each of kelp and licorice, and 0.3 grams of aconite, decocted in water for oral administration. This formula is a miraculous medicine to dissolve phlegm in the upper burner. Seaweed and kelp help remove external signs of the goiter and eliminate the strange colorful patterns. The key is to resolve phlegm without damaging qi, thereby keeping the stomach qi strong and facilitating the transformation of phlegm. With one dose, one knows; two doses can eliminate most of it; three doses can completely dissolve it; and four doses will prevent recurrence. This formula can also treat goiter symptoms and is remarkably effective.

If a person suddenly has swelling and pain in the throat, accompanied by double eyelids, such that they cannot eat, they could die within five days without food. However, this condition of real fire is easier to treat. For real fire, one can use mountain bean root, and herbs like qin (skullcap), lian (lotus), banxia, chaihu (bupleurum), licorice, platycodon, and tianhuafeng (trichosanthes) for immediate relief. Yet, the condition of false fire occurs when kidney fire does not settle in the mingmen (life gate) but floats between the throat. Its symptoms resemble those of real fire, but are heavier at night and lighter in the morning. Conversely, with real fire, symptoms are heavier in the morning and lighter at night. Real fire causes dryness and cracking in the mouth; false fire does not create much thirst but shows a slippery tongue without cracks. Use this method of distinguishing symptoms to avoid mistakes.[83p]

此等虚痛，若亦以治实火之法治之，是人已下井，而又益之石也。故不特不可用寒凉，并不可用发散，盖虚火必须补也。然徒补肾水，虽水能制火，可以少差，而火热太盛，未易制伏。又宜于水中补火，则引火归原，而火势顿消亡于顷刻矣。方用引火汤，熟地、元参各一两，白芥子三钱，山茱萸、山药各四钱，北五味、肉桂各二钱，茯苓五钱，水煎服一剂，而痰声静，痛顿除，肿亦尽消；二剂全愈。盖熟地、山茱萸、五味之类，纯是补肾水圣药；茯苓、山药又益精而利水，助肉桂之下行；元参以消在上之浮火；白芥子以消壅塞之痰。上焦既宽而下焦又得肉桂之热，则龙雷之火，有不归根于命门者乎？一剂便生。真有鬼神莫测之机，又胜于八味地黄汤也。倘喉肿闭塞，勺水不能下，此方将安施乎？更有一法，用附子一个，破故纸五钱，各研末，调如糊，作膏，布摊如膏药，大如茶锺，贴脚心中央，以火烘之，一时辰，喉即宽而开一线路，可以服药矣。[84p]

These虚痛s (false pains), if treated with methods meant for real fire, are like a person who has fallen into a well and then adds stones to it. Therefore, not only should one avoid cold and cooling treatments, but one should also refrain from using dispersing methods, as虚火 (false fire) must be supplemented. However, merely supplementing kidney water, while water can control fire, may only alleviate the situation slightly, as the fire is too intense and hard to subdue. It is better to supplement fire with water, leading the fire back to its original source, causing its force to vanish in an instant. One should use the Y引火 Decoction: prepared Rehmannia and Fritillaria (each 1 tael), white mustard seed (3 qian), Chinese dogwood and yam (each 4 qian), northern spices and cinnamon (each 2 qian), poria (5 qian), then decoct with water and take as a dose, which will calm the phlegm, relieve the pain, and eliminate the swelling; two doses will bring complete recovery. The prepared Rehmannia, Chinese dogwood, and spices primarily reinforce kidney water; poria and yam also benefit essence and facilitate water, assisting the descent of cinnamon; Fritillaria dissipates the floating fire above; while white mustard seeds eliminate obstructive phlegm. Once the upper focus is relaxed and the lower focus receives the warmth of cinnamon, is there any chance that the fire of the dragon and thunder will not return to its root in the mingmen? One dose is effective. The unpredictable workings of spirits and ghosts are even better than the Eight-Flavored Rehmannia Decoction. If the throat is swollen and blocked, and not even a spoonful of water can be swallowed, how will this formula be applied? Furthermore, there is another method: use one piece of aconite, five qian of broken old paper, ground into powder, mix into a paste, shape it into a patch as large as a teacup, apply it to the center of the sole, and warm it with fire for a while. After one period, the throat will widen, opening a pathway to take medicine.[84p]

　　　　　乳蛾

　　更有人病双蛾者，人以为热也。喉门肿痛，痰如锯不绝，茶水一滴不能下咽，岂非热证？然而痛虽甚，至早少轻；喉虽肿，舌必不燥；痰虽多，必不黄而成块。此乃假热之证也。若以寒凉之药急救之，下喉非不暂快，少顷而热转甚。人以为凉药之少也，再加寒凉之品，服之更甚。急须刺其少商之穴出血少许，喉门必有一线之路开矣。急以附子一钱，熟地一两，山茱萸四钱，麦冬、北五味、牛膝各三钱，茯苓五钱，煎服下喉，一声响喨，其火势热证立时消散。[85p]

Moth of Milk

There are some who suffer from a dual moth condition, which others mistakenly attribute to heat. The throat swells painfully, phlegm incessantly thick like sawdust, and not a single drop of tea can be swallowed. Isn’t this a sign of heat? Yet, despite the intense pain, it becomes somewhat lighter by morning; although the throat is swollen, the tongue will not be dry; although there is abundant phlegm, it will not be yellow and clotted. This is a sign of false heat. If one hastily uses cold and cool medicines for urgent relief, it may seem to soothe the throat momentarily, but soon the heat intensifies even more. People assume that the cooling medicine was insufficient and add more cold remedies, which only aggravates the condition. It is urgent to prick the Shaoshang point to draw a little blood; this will surely open a line of passage in the throat. It is essential to use one qian of Aconite, one liang of Rehmannia, four qian of Cornus, three qian each of Ophiopogon, Chinese Amomum, and Achyranthes, and five qian of Poria; decoct and administer down the throat, and a sound shall resonate, causing the fiery heat to dissipate immediately.[85p]

盖少阴之火，直如奔马，凡人肾水大耗者，肾中元阳不能下藏，盖无水以养火，而火必上越也。日日冲上而咽喉口小，不能任其出入，乃结成肿痛，状似双蛾，实非双蛾也。方中妙在用附子辛热之药，引龙雷之火，下藏于窟宅。夫龙雷之火，乃相火也，喜水而不喜火，故药中熟地、山茱之类，纯是补阴之味，使火有所归而不再沸，此因其逆势而逆导之。然喜水者，喜真阴之水也，而非寒凉之水；不喜火者，不喜邪气之火也，而非辛热之火。至若日重夜轻，治之最易。[86p]

The fire of the Lesser Yin is like a galloping horse. When a person loses a significant amount of kidney water, the original Yang in the kidneys cannot settle down, as there is no water to nourish the fire, which must then rise. Daily, it surges upward and constricts the throat, making it unable to properly function, leading to swellings and pains resembling double moths, though they are not actually double moths. The key lies in using spicy and warm drugs like aconite to guide the fire of the dragon and thunder down into the dwelling. The fire of the dragon and thunder represents the fire of the heart; it enjoys water but dislikes fire. Therefore, herbs like cooked rehmannia and shan zhu yu, which are purely nourishing for Yin, are used to give the fire a place to return, preventing it from boiling over. This is due to counteracting its reverse tendencies. What it enjoys is the true Yin water, not the cold and cooling type; what it dislikes is the fire of邪气 (xieqi), not the spicy and warm fire. As for the condition of having heavier days and lighter nights, it is the easiest to treat.[86p]

用山豆根、桔梗各三钱，半夏、甘草各一钱，治之一剂立愈，而非逆证可比耳。　　阴虚双蛾之证，更有治法。用附子一钱，盐水炒成片，用一片含在口中，立时有路可以用汤药矣。后以八味丸一两，白滚水送下，亦立时可愈。　　又双蛾阴证，最难治而最易治也。不知其窍而最难，知其法而最易。予常为人治此病，用附子一枚，以盐一合，水煮透，令其口含一片，而火势立止，然后以六味汤大剂饮之，不再发，神方也。[87p]

Using three qian of mountain bean root and balloon flower, and one qian each of pinellia and licorice, a single dose will cure immediately, provided it is not a case of reverse syndrome. For the symptoms of dual moths with yin deficiency, there are additional methods of treatment. Use one qian of aconite, fried with salt water into pieces; hold one piece in the mouth to immediately enable the use of decoction. Then, take one liang of Eight Flavor Pill with boiling water, and it can also cure immediately.

Moreover, the yin syndrome of dual moths is both the most difficult and the easiest to treat. Not knowing the key makes it very hard, but knowing the method makes it very easy. I often treat this illness using one piece of aconite, with one he of salt, boiled in water until thoroughly cooked, allowing the patient to hold one piece in the mouth, after which the fire will stop; then, take a large dose of Six Flavor Decoction, and it will not recur—this is a divine formula.[87p]

　　阴蛾之证，乃肾水亏乏，火不能藏于下，乃飞越于上，而喉中关狭，火不得直泄，乃结成蛾，似蛾而非蛾也。早晨痛轻，下午痛重，至黄昏而痛更甚。得热则快，得凉则加。其证之重者，滴水不能下喉。若作外感阳证治之，用山豆根、芩、连、栀子之类，则痛益甚而关不开，有不尽命而死者矣。惟补阴虚，用引火归原之法，而痛顿失也，方名化蛾丹，熟地、山茱萸、麦冬各一两，附子一钱，车前子三钱，北五味二钱，水煎服。此方大补肾之水，不治蛾之痛，壮水则火息，引火则痛消，故一剂即可收功，奇绝之法也。古今图书集成医部全录卷一百六十二[88p]

The condition of the "yin moth" is due to a deficiency of kidney water, where the fire cannot be contained below and thus rises above. The throat is narrow, preventing the fire from being released directly, resulting in the formation of a "moth," which resembles a moth but is not. The pain is lighter in the morning and heavier in the afternoon, exacerbating by dusk. It is relieved by heat and worsened by coolness. In severe cases, even a drop of water cannot go down the throat. If treated as an external wind-heat condition using herbs like mountain soy root, qin (scutellaria), lian (lotus), and gardenia, the pain may increase and the throat will remain obstructed, potentially leading to death. Only by nourishing the yin deficiency and employing methods that redirect fire to its source can the pain be alleviated. This is known as the "Transforming Moth Pill," consisting of one liang each of reheated land (shudihuang), shanzhu yu (cornelian cherry), and mai dong (ophiopogon), along with 1 qian of fu zi (prepared aconite) and 3 qians of che qian zi (plantago) and 2 qians of bei wu wei zi (schisandra). These ingredients are decocted in water for ingestion. This formula greatly nourishes the kidney water, rather than treating the pain of the "moth." Strengthening the water will quell the fire; thus, the pain dissipates, making this method exceptionally effective.[88p]

Throat Gateway

Prescription

Jingfang Baidu Powder
Jing Jie Suan, Fang Feng, Qiang Huo, Du Huo, Chai Hu, Qian Hu, Chuan Xiong, Zhi Ke, Jie Geng, Fu Ling, each one tael; Gan Cao five qian. Take one tael each time, add three slices of fresh ginger and a little mint, and decoct.

Qing Yan Li Ge Decoction
For treating accumulated heat causing swollen and painful throat, with phlegm and saliva congestion. Jin Yin Hua, Fang Feng, Jing Jie, Mint, Jie Geng, Huang Qin (stir-fried), Huang Lian (stir-fried), half a qian each; Shan Zhi, Lian Qiao, two qian each; Yuan Shen, Da Huang (stewed), (Shi Bu) Nitrate, Niu Bang Zi (burdock seeds) ground, Gan Cao, each seven fen. Prepare a dose with two sheng of water, decoct to one sheng, and take after meals. Removing Jin Yin Hua from this formula yields the Qing Xin Li Ge Decoction, treating the same condition.

Golden Key
For treating closed throat with excess phlegm and saliva, making it hard to swallow liquids. Combine half a sheng of fire nitrate, five qian of borax, a character of brain powder, two qian of realgar, and one qian of white silkworm, each ground separately and mixed. Blow the mixture onto the affected area with a bamboo tube; phlegm and saliva will be expelled. If phlegm is expelled but the throat remains blocked, needle the affected area to remove bad blood.[89p]

Liangge San: Treats throat obstruction.
Ingredients: Huangqin (scutellaria), wine-fried; Zhizi (gardenia), fried; Bohe (mint), each one liang; Lianqiao (forsythia), four liang; Dahuang (rhubarb), soaked in wine; Mangxiao (mirabilite), Gancao (licorice), each two liang. Grind together into a powder; take five qian each time.

Fangfeng Tongsheng San: Treats throat obstruction and throat abscess.

Buzhong Yiqi Tang: Treats the aforementioned conditions that belong to qi deficiency.

Sishen Tang: Treats the aforementioned conditions that belong to blood deficiency.
Ingredients: Danggui (angelica), washed with wine; Shudi (reheated rehmannia), each three qian; Chuanxiong (ligusticum), washed with wine, one qian and five fen; Baishao (white peony), fried with wine, two qian. Decoction with water; take warm.

Qing Wei San treats damp-heat in the stomach channel, swelling and pain in the teeth and throat, which may pull on the head or cause facial heat, and it addresses these issues.

Jing Jie Decoction is for treating swelling and pain in the throat, inability to speak, and severe pain when swallowing.

Bi Xue is used for all kinds of accumulated heat, sores on the mouth and tongue, irritability and throat constriction, and pain in the teeth and gums.

Prepare a decoction of Licorice with two sheng of water, add the other herbs and decoct again, stirring continuously with a willow branch until melted. Pour into a sand basin and let it cool to form frost, then grind the frost into a powder. Use a small amount to dissolve and swallow. If the throat is constricted to the point of inability to swallow, use a bamboo tube to blow the medicine into the throat.

Po Guan Dan treats the closure of the throat due to phlegm, throat constriction, and related symptoms.

　　瓜蒂散　治缠喉风，咽中如束气不通。　　瓜蒂不拘多少
　　右细研为末，壮年一字，十五岁已上及年老者服半字，早晨用井华水调下，一时须含砂糖一块，良久涎如水出。年深者涎尽，有一块如石，布水上如鉴。涎尽，食粥一二日。如吐多困甚，即咽麝香汤一盏。麝香须细研，用温水调下。此药不大吐逆，只吐涎水。又瓜蒂须采自然，落者用如未用，以槟榔叶裹于东墙有风处，挂令吹干用。[95p]

Seven Treasures Powder: For treating throat constriction and wind constricting the throat.
Ten silkworms, borax, realgar, alum, scorpions (to detoxify), and one stick of pig's tooth pod, peeled and strung, each one qian; half a qian of copper sulfate. Grind these into a fine powder. Use one character at a time, blow it into the throat, and it will heal.

Thousand Threads Decoction: For treating the above conditions.
Seven pieces of pinellia, one inch of soap pod and licorice, all roasted, boiled with ginger and jujubes.

Five Spices Powder: For treating swollen sore throat, blockage of foul air. It is urgently needed.
One tael each of wood aromatics, agarwood, chicken tongue herb, and fragrant earth; three fen of musk. Grind these into a fine powder, mix well. Take two qian, with one cup of water, boil until down to one-half, and take warm as desired.

Melon Stem Powder: For treating wind constricting the throat, causing a sensation of binding air in the throat.
The quantity of melon stems is not fixed. Grind the melon stems finely into powder; adults take one character, and those over fifteen or elderly take half a character. In the morning, mix with well water and take with a piece of sugar to hold in the mouth; after a long time, saliva will flow like water. For those who have deepened conditions, if the saliva diminishes, there will be a piece like stone; if it is floated or looks like a mirror on water, when the saliva is gone, eat congee for one or two days. If too much is vomited and it is troubling, drink a cup of musk decoction. The musk must be finely ground and mixed with warm water. This medicine does not cause severe vomiting, only the expulsion of saliva. Furthermore, the melon stems must be harvested naturally; those that have fallen are to be used without utilizing them. Wrap them in betel palm leaves and hang them to dry in a windy area against the east wall.[95p]

　　乌犀膏　治咽喉肿痛，一切结喉烂喉，遁尸，缠喉，痹喉，急喉，飞丝入喉，重舌，木舌等证。　　皂夹两条，椎碎，用水三升，浸一时，久挼汁去滓，入瓦器内，熬成膏　好酒一合　焰硝　百草霜研，各一钱，同皂角膏搅匀令稠　人参一钱，为末　硼砂　白霜梅各少许，并研入膏中。　　右拌和前药，用鹅毛点少许于喉中，以出尽顽涎为度，却嚼甘草二寸，咽汁吞津。
　　备急如圣散　治时气缠喉风，渐入咽喉闭塞，水谷不下，牙关紧急，不省人事。　　雄黄细研，生用　藜芦厚者去皮，生用　白矾飞　猪牙皂角去皮弦　　右，等分为细末，每用一豆大，鼻内(口畜)之，立效。
　　一字散　治喉闭气塞不通，饮食不下。　　雄黄研　白矾生研　藜芦各一钱　蝎梢七枚　猪牙皂角七挺　　右为末，每用一字，吹入鼻中，即时吐出顽涎，愈。[96p]

Wu Xi Gao: Treats swollen and painful throats, including all forms of throat obstruction and ulceration, such as hidden corpse, throat binding, throat numbness, urgent throat issues, flying threads entering the throat, heavy tongue, wooden tongue, and similar conditions.

Take two pieces of soapberry, crush them, soak in three sheng (a volume measure) of water for one period, repeatedly knead to extract the juice and discard the residue, then place into a pottery vessel and boil down to a paste. Add one cup of good wine, a pinch of saltpeter, and one qian each of powdered herb frost, mix well to thicken, along with one qian of powdered ginseng. Add a small amount of borax and white plum frost, and grind into the paste.

Combine the preceding ingredients, use a goose feather to apply a small amount to the throat until the stubborn phlegm is expelled, then chew two inches of licorice, swallow the juice and saliva.

Bei Ji Ru Sheng San: Treats seasonal throat wind afflictions, gradually obstructing the throat and preventing food and water from going down, with tightly clenched teeth and loss of consciousness.

Finely grind realgar and use raw. For thick raphanus, remove the skin and use raw. Burned alum, and prepare the pig's tooth soapberry by removing the skin and string.

Combine these into fine powder, using equal parts, take a bean-sized quantity and place it in the nostrils (or mouth), immediate results are seen.

Yi Zi San: Treats throat closure, air blockage, and inability to ingest food and drink.

Grind realgar, raw alum, and raphanus each one qian, add seven scorpion tails and seven pieces of pig's tooth soapberry.

Grind together, take a word-sized amount, blow it into the nose, and stubborn phlegm will be expelled immediately, leading to recovery.[96p]

Two parts Coptis, two parts Scutellaria, two parts Rhubarb, prepared with nine steams and nine sun-dryings. Mix equally, form into honey pills the size of tung seeds, adjusting the quantity based on the patient's condition of deficiency or excess.

Dragon and Musk Gathering Sacred Pill for treating heart and spleen heat, toxic qi attacking the throat, causing redness, swelling, and pain; it may lead to throat paralysis or hard masses that do not dissolve, recurring after recovery, with a persistent condition; also for swollen tongue base, mouth ulcers, and difficulty swallowing food and drink.

Detoxifying Niu Huang Pill

For treating both adults and children: sore throat, stiff tongue, ulcers throughout the mouth, excessive salivation, urgent wheezing, difficulty in eating, and obstruction in the chest.

Ingredients:

  • 3.5 qian Niu Huang (Bovine bile)
  • 5 qian each of: Ren Shen (Ginseng), Nan Hu Po (Amber), fine powder of Xi Jiao (Rhinoceros horn), Jie Geng (Platycodon), Sheng Di Huang (Rehmannia), and Borax
  • 1 liang Xiong Huang (Realgar), water-floated
  • 3 qian each of Yuan Shen (Dipsacus) and Sheng Ma (Cimicifuga)
  • 4 liang He Fen (Conch powder), water-floated
  • 1 qian each of Qian Bai Shuang (Lead white) and Pian Nao (Alum)
  • 2 liang Han Shui Shi (Calamine), calcined
  • 7 qian Zhu Sha (Cinnabar), ground and floated

These ingredients are to be finely powdered, shaped into pills the size of small pellets, coated with gold leaf, and stored in a porcelain container. Each dose consists of one pill, taken with a strong decoction of mint tea, or with freshly drawn water. Take 2-3 doses daily after meals, and it can also be dissolved in the mouth.[98p]

Dried Ginger Powder
Treats hanging sores that suddenly swell and heat up.
Dried ginger and half summer (Ban Xia) are washed to remove the slickness, equally divided.
Grind these into a fine powder and place a small amount on the tongue to swallow.

Yuan Shen Powder
Treats hanging sores accompanied by pain and loss of appetite.
Equal parts of Sheng Ma, She Gan, and Da Huang (each half a tael), with two and a half qian of Gan Cao and one tael of Yuan Shen.
Grind into a fine powder, decoct in water until reduced to seven parts, let cool, and hold in the mouth to swallow. It is very effective.

She Gan Pills
Treats swelling and pain of hanging sores and difficulty in the throat.
Wash apricot seeds, removing skins, tips, and double seeds, then lightly roast with bran until slightly yellow, and combine with equal parts of roasted Gan Cao and She Gan.
Also, lightly stir-fry Sheng Ma and Da Huang, and half a qian each of Mu Bie Zi.
Grind these into a fine powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of a ball, and often keep one in the mouth to swallow.

Salt and Alum Powder
Treats hanging sore in the throat that is long and obstructive, causing a feeling of heaviness.
Burn salt and dry white alum.
Grind finely, mix in equal parts. Apply with the tip of a chopstick and it will dissolve.

She Gan Pills
Treats swelling and pain of hanging sores, difficulty in the throat, and heat in the chest.

Borosilicate powder, for treating swelling and pain of hanging sores.

Grind two qian each of borosilicate, Ma Ya salt, talcum powder, and cold water stone; grind half a qian of powdered brain; one and a half qian of white alum. This mixture should be made into a fine powder. Each use is half a qian, taken at any time with fresh spring water.

Qi Guan powder, for treating wind-heat invading the upper burner, causing swelling and pain from hanging sores.

Roast two liang of bitter herbs and use fresh licorice. This should also be made into a fine powder. Each dose is two qian, used with one cup of water, decocted for six minutes, then swish in the mouth for a long time before swallowing.

Huang Qi powder, for treating throat sores and pain.

Half a liang each of Huang Qi, betel nut, purple aster (washed), burdock seed, gardenia seed, red poria, and fresh licorice; three qian each of Cimicifuga and Scutellaria; one liang each of Yuanshen and Ophiopogon. Grind finely. Each dose is one qian with one cup of water, decocted down to six minutes, then strain and take.

Tao Hong powder, for treating sores and swelling in the throat, presenting red-purple coloration, causing pain that hinders swallowing.

Ten pieces each of gold and silver foil, a little lead white frost, four liang of cold water stone, and two liang of Taiyin original essence stone. These two ingredients should be crushed, placed into a container, fired until they turn red, then buried in the ground to release heat toxins, and ground finely.

Grind one liang each of Ma Ya salt, cinnabar, and roasted licorice into a fine powder. Each dose is one character's worth mixed with licorice water; alternatively, make small pills the size of peas using thin glutinous rice porridge, hold in the mouth to dissolve and swallow.[103p]

Amber and rhinoceros horn ointment treats sores in the throat, mouth, and tongue caused by pathogens. Genuine amber is ground with rhinoceros horn shavings, each one qian, along with raw ginseng (with the husk removed), sour jujube seeds (with the husk removed), and cultivable red cinnabar, each two qian. Life-saving powder treats heat toxins in the spleen and stomach that ascend and cause sores in the throat, along with phlegm in the throat. Use three qian of greasy powder, two and a half qian of cinquefoil, chopped rhubarb (stir-fried), yellow root, and white silkworms (stir-fried), each half a liang of raw licorice. Vomiting means survival; if not vomiting, the outcome is death.[104p]

　　牛蒡子丸　治咽喉内热毒所攻生疮肿痛。　　牛蒡子一两，微炒　升麻　黄药子　干浮萍草　元参　甘草生，各半两　　右为细末，炼蜜和丸，如弹子大，常噙一丸咽津。
　　硼砂散　治心脾风热所发，咽喉生疮肿痛，或子舌胀，或木舌重舌，肿闷闭塞，水浆不下。　　硼砂研，三两　薄荷叶　蒲黄各一两　青黛研　贯众　元参　茯苓　缩砂　滑石研　荆芥穗　山豆根　甘草生，各半两　寒水石煅研，二两半　　右为细末，研匀，每服半钱不拘时，用新汲水调下。
　　半夏厚朴汤　一名加味四七汤，治前证。　　紫苏叶　半夏　厚朴　赤茯苓　陈皮　枳实　南星　缩砂　神曲各一钱　青皮七分　槟榔　益智仁各三分　白豆蔻六分　姜五片　水煎服。[105p]

Burdock Seed Pills: Treats sores and swelling in the throat caused by heat and toxins. Use one ounce of burdock seeds, lightly roasted; half an ounce each of angelica, yellow medicine, dried duckweed, root of Scrophularia, and raw licorice. Grind all to a fine powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of a marble, and orally dissolve one pill to swallow saliva regularly.

Borax Powder: Treats sores and swelling in the throat caused by wind-heat affecting the heart and spleen, which may lead to swelling of the tongue or thickened tongue with obstruction preventing liquid intake. Grind three ounces of borax; one ounce each of mint leaves and cattail pollen; half an ounce each of indigo, plantain, Scrophularia, poria, sand, talc, and Schizonepeta spikes; half an ounce each of mountain bean root and raw licorice. Prepare two and a half ounces of calcined cold water stone; mix all into a fine powder. Take half a penny’s worth at any time, dissolved in freshly drawn water.

Banxia Houpu Decoction, also known as Enhanced Four-Seven Decoction, treats preceding symptoms. Ingredients: one penny each of perilla leaves, pinellia, magnolia bark, red poria, dried tangerine peel, bitter orange fruit, south star, sand; seven-tenths of a penny of green peel; three-tenths each of betel nut and amomum; six-tenths of a penny of white cardamom; five slices of ginger. Boil with water for consumption.[105p]

　　射干散　治咽喉中如有物妨，闷噎塞疼痛，咽物不下。　　射干　桔梗　川升麻　犀角屑，各三钱　木香　木通各半两　紫苏子炒　诃黎勒去核　槟榔　枳壳去穰，麸炒　赤茯苓　甘草炙，各一两　　右銼细末，每服三钱，水一盏，煎至八分，去滓，不拘时温服。
　　含化龙脑丸　治咽喉中有物如弹丸，日数深远津液难咽，作渴疼痛，即须深针肿结处，散尽毒气。　　龙脑研　麝香研，各二钱半　锺乳粉　马牙硝　升麻　黄芪各一两　大黄炒　炙甘草各半两　生地黄五两，取汁和药　　右为细末，研匀，以地黄汁更入炼蜜和丸，如弹子大，不拘时以绵裹一丸噙化咽津，以咽喉通利为度。
　　木香散　治咽喉中如有物噎塞，吞不能入，吐不能出。　　木香半两　紫雪　射干　羚羊角屑　犀角屑　槟榔各一两　元参　桑白皮　升麻各一两半　　右銼碎，每服三钱，水一盏，煎至六分，去滓，不拘时温服。[106p]

Shegan San: Treats the sensation of something obstructing the throat, causing discomfort, choking, and pain, making swallowing difficult. Ingredients: Shegan, Jiegeng, Chuan Shengma, rhino horn powder—each 9 grams; Muxiang, Mutong—each 15 grams; Zisuzi (stir-fried), He Li Le (pitted), Betel nut, Zhike (husks removed and stir-fried), Chiffonized Polyporus (Fu Ling), and honey-roasted licorice—each 30 grams. Grind to a fine powder. For each dose, take 9 grams, mix with one cup of water, and simmer until reduced to 80%. Strain and take warm at any time.

Long Nao Wan: Treats the sensation of a round object in the throat, causing difficulty in swallowing saliva, thirst, and pain. It requires deep needling of swollen areas to dispel toxic qi. Ingredients: Long Nao (dragon brain), musk—each 7.5 grams; Congruent essential powder, Ma Ya Xiao, Sheng Ma, Huang Qi—each 30 grams; stir-fried Dahuang and honey-roasted licorice—each 15 grams; Sheng Di Huang—250 grams, extract the juice and mix with the medicine. Grind into a fine powder, mix well, and use the Di Huang juice to form pills the size of pellets. Take as needed, wrapped in cotton to dissolve in saliva to promote throat comfort.

Muxiang San: Treats the sensation of something obstructing the throat, making swallowing impossible and expulsion difficult. Ingredients: Muxiang—15 grams; Zixue, Shegan, Antelope horn powder, rhino horn powder, Betel nut—each 30 grams; Yuanshen, Sangbai Pi, Sheng Ma—each 45 grams. Grind finely; for each dose, take 9 grams, mix with one cup of water, simmer until reduced to 60%. Strain and take warm at any time.[106p]

　　络石汤　治咽喉中如有物噎塞。
　　络石　紫菀各半两　升麻　射干各七钱半　木通　赤茯苓　桔梗炒，各一两　　右銼碎，每服五钱匕，水一盏半，煎至八分，去滓，食后温服。如要通利，及汤成，加芒硝末一钱匕，搅匀服之。络石即石薜荔。
　　四味汤　治咽喉中如有物，咽吐不利。　　半夏以生姜汁浸一宿，汤浸切洗　厚朴刮去粗皮，以生姜汁浸，炙黄　橘皮以汤浸去白，焙，各一两　赤茯苓刮去黑皮，二两　　右銼碎，每服三钱匕，水一盏，入姜一大枣劈破，煎至六分去滓，食远温服。
　　杏仁煎丸　治咽喉食即噎塞，如有物不下。　　杏仁汤浸，去皮尖及双仁，炒，半两　官桂去粗皮　枇杷叶拭去毛，炙　人参各一两　　右为细末，炼蜜为丸，如樱桃大，每服一丸，含化咽津，以瘥为度。[107p]

Luo Shi Decoction: Treats the sensation of an obstructive mass in the throat.
Luo Shi and Zi Wan, each half a tael; Sheng Ma and She Gan, each seven and a half qian; Mu Tong, Chi Fu Ling, and Jie Geng, stir-fried, each one tael. Pound all and finely grind. Take five qian with a ladle of water, decoct until reduced to eight portions, strain, and take warm after meals. If needed for unblocking, add one qian of Mangxiao powder to the decoction, mix well and consume. Luo Shi refers to Shi Bei Li.

Si Wei Decoction: Treats sensation of obstruction in the throat, with difficulty swallowing and spitting.
Ban Xia soaked overnight in ginger juice, then washed and sliced; Hou Po scraped to remove the coarse skin, soaked in ginger juice and roasted until yellow; Chen Pi soaked in broth to remove the white part and then toasted, all one tael. Chi Fu Ling, scraped to remove black skin, two taels. Pound all and finely grind. Take three qian with a ladle of water, add one large piece of ginger and a jujube, broken, decoct until reduced to six portions, strain, and take warm before meals.

Apricot Kernel Decoction Pills: Treats obstruction in the throat where food cannot go down, as if there is a mass stuck.
Apricot kernels soaked in decoction, with the skin tip and double kernels removed, roasted, half a tael; Guan Gui with coarse skin removed; Loquat leaves wiped clean of fuzz, roasted; Ren Shen each one tael. Grind all into a fine powder, combine with honey to make pills the size of cherries. Take one pill, hold in the mouth to dissolve and swallow saliva, adjusting based on recovery.[107p]

　　射干麻黄汤　治前证。

Gancao Xiexin Decoction: Treats the previous symptoms. Ingredients: Huangqin, Renshen, Ganjiang, each 3 taels; 12 Da Zao, split; Banxia, 0.5 sheng; Gancao, 4 taels; Huanglian, 1 tael. Combine these seven ingredients with 10 dou of water, boil to extract 6 sheng, then remove the residue, reboil, and take 1 sheng warm, three times a day.

Kushen Decoction: Treats Huohuo disease; parasites in the lower body cause dryness in the throat. Ingredients: Kushen, 0.5 jin; Huai Baipi, Wolf's Tooth Root, each 4 taels. Grind these, add 5 sheng of water, boil down to 3.5 sheng, and wash the lower body.

Xiaojianzhong Decoction: Treats the previous symptoms. Ingredients: Guizhi, Zhizhi Gancao, each 3 taels; 12 Da Zao; Shaoyao, 6 taels; Shengjiang, 3 taels; Jiao Yi, 1 sheng. Combine these six ingredients with 7 sheng of water, boil the first five ingredients, take 3 sheng, remove the residue, add Jiao Yi, and simmer gently to dissolve. Take 1 sheng warm, three times a day.

Shegan Mahuang Decoction: Treats the previous symptoms. Ingredients: Shegan, 13 pieces; Mahuang, 4 taels; Shengjiang, 4 taels; Xixin, Zihuan, and Donghua, each 3 taels; Wuweizi, 0.5 sheng; large Banxia, wash and use 8 pieces; 7 Da Zao. Combine these nine ingredients with 12.2 dou of water, first boil Mahuang, remove the foam, add the other herbs, and boil to get 3 sheng. Divide into three warm doses. Some sources suggest using 3 taels of Shegan and 0.5 sheng of Banxia.[108p]

　　如圣胜金锭 【《局方》】 　治咽喉急闭，并单蛾、双蛾、结喉、重舌、木舌等证。　　硫黄　川芎　腊茶　脑薄荷　川乌　生地黄　硝石　各等分为末，生葱汁和匀，一两分作十锭。每取一锭，先以凉水灌漱，次嚼薄荷五七叶，却用药同嚼，以井水咽下。甚者连进三服。[109p]

Shengma Bie Jia Decoction, also known as Shu Jiao Decoction, treats the above-mentioned conditions.

  • Ingredients:
    • 1 tael of Dang Gui,
    • 2 taels each of Sheng Ma and Gan Cao (Licorice),
    • One piece of Bie Jia the size of a finger, roasted,
    • 0.5 tael of Xiong Huang (Realgar), ground.

Mix these six ingredients with 4 sheng of water, boil down to 1 sheng, and take as a single dose; elders and children should take it again to induce sweating.

Mai Men Dong Decoction treats the above-mentioned conditions.

  • Ingredients:
    • 7 sheng of Mai Men Dong (Ophiopogon),
    • 1 sheng of Ban Xia (Pinellia),
    • 2 taels each of Ren Shen (Ginseng) and Gan Cao,
    • 3 heaping cups of Jing Mi (Glutinous Rice),
    • 12 large jujubes.

Boil these six ingredients in 12 sheng of water until 6 sheng remain. Take 1 sheng warm, three times during the day and once at night.

For the Sacred Victory Gold Tablets [from the "Jufang"], this treats acute closure of the throat, as well as conditions linked with single and double moths, tight throat, heavy tongue, and wooden tongue.

  • Ingredients:
    • Equal parts of Sulfur, Chuan Xiong (Szechuan Lovage), La Tea, Brain Mint, Chuan Wu (Black Aconite), Sheng Di Huang (Raw Rehmannia), and Niter, ground to a powder.

Mix with fresh green onion juice, dividing into ten tablets of 1 tael each. For use, take one tablet, first gargle with cool water, then chew 5-7 leaves of mint, and continue chewing the medicine with the mint before swallowing with well water. In severe cases, take three doses in succession.[109p]

Er Xian San (Two Immortals Powder)
For treating acute throat closure and severe throat wind.
One qian of alum and three qian of white silkworms.
Grind these into a powder and blow a small amount into the throat.

Niu Huang Liang Ge Wan (Cattle Gall Cooling Pill)
For treating swollen and painful throat, sores in the mouth and tongue, swollen cheeks, and heat phlegm obstruction.
Two liang of each of the following: maiyaxiao, cold water stone burnt, and gypsum burnt; seven and a half qian of cattle gall; five qian of burnt purple quartz; two and a half qian each of dragon brain, musk, and cattle gall; one liang of honey-fried licorice.
Grind all into a powder, mix with honey, making thirty pills, each to be chewed down with peppermint tea.

Duo Ming San (Life-Stealing Powder)
For treating acute throat closure.
Equal parts of dried white alum, fried white silkworms, borax, and soap pod.
Grind these into a powder and blow a small amount into the throat; phlegm will be expelled immediately.

Dan Huang San (Gall Powder)
For treating throat obstruction and swelling.
Half a qian of alum and two whole scorpions.
Grind these into a powder, use a chicken feather dipped in the medicine to place in the throat, and shortly after a sound will break forth; then use fresh lotus leaves ground finely, mixed with well water, and swallow; expelling toxic saliva will result in healing; if not expelled, take again.[110p]

Chicken Inner Gold Powder (Danxi)
Treats throat congestion, both single and double moth.
In the twelfth month, dry the chicken's inner gold, grind finely into powder, one qian. Add three qian of mung bean powder. Mix with honey to form three pills. Dissolve in the mouth for remarkable effects.

Dragon Brain Ointment (Jufang)
Treats throat phlegm, swelling, and pain.
Take five grains of sand, one pound of peppermint leaves, three taels of licorice, two taels each of saposhnikovia, chuanxiong, and platycodon, one tael of nitrate, one qian of brain powder, and thirty grains of cardamom. Grind into powder, form honey pills the size of a marble, dissolve in the mouth and swallow.

Green Dragon Gall (Huoren)
Treats throat blockage and swelling, effective for both single and double moth.
Copper sulfate placed in the gall of a green fish, dried into powder, blown into the throat for immediate results. If there is no green fish, substitute with the gall of a carp. Best in the twelfth month.

Throat Blowing Powder (Gangmu)
Treats swollen and blocked throat.
Five qian of copper sulfate, if unavailable, substitute with green vitriol, put into the gall of a green fish, wind-dried; if no green fish, use the gall of a carp. Seven shelled snake beans, one qian of copper blue, two and a half qian of nitrate, ground separately. Five fen of light powder and one character of indigo. Mix the copper sulfate with the snake beans in a copper pan, remove the snake beans, combine with the other four ingredients, add a little musk. Use one character to blow into the throat, expectorate phlegm and blood, and recover immediately.[111p]

Qingliang San [from "Huichun", same below]
Treats real fire causing sore throat and swelling.

Jiawei Siwu Decoction
Treats deficient fire causing throat obstruction, throat pain, throat sores, most effective in reducing fire.

Longnao Podu San
Treats rapid and chronic throat obstruction with swelling and blockage.

Jin Suoji [from "Yijian"]
Treats acute throat obstruction and throat wind.

Bai Fan San
Treats sore throat wind and acute throat closure.
Three qian of alum, three seeds of croton, shelled and divided into six pieces. Roasted together in a pan until the alum is dry; remove the seeds and grind the alum into a powder, dissolve in water to take orally; or blow into the throat; or mix with chicken egg white and administer into the throat.

Chui Hou San
Treats hanging abscess, swelling pain, and all throat ailments.
Copper sulfate, alum, quicklime, fragments of brain, mountain bean root, cinnabar, roasted chicken inner golden. Grind to a very fine powder and use a bamboo tube to blow a small amount into the throat for immediate effect.

Jia Wei Er Chen Tang
Treats plum kernel qi.
Two qian each of ginseng, roasted atractylodes, dried tangerine peel, white poria, and pinellia; five fen of prepared licorice; seven fen each of bitter orange peel, ballota, scute, gardenia seeds, perilla seeds, and white cardamom. Grate to make one dose, add three slices of ginger, and decoct in water for oral administration.

Niu Bang Zi Tang
Treats sore throat, tight jaws; may cause sores and abscesses; or relapse after recovery attacking the chest and flanks, causing shortness of breath and body heat, unable to sit or lie down.
Two qian of burdock seeds, each one qian of root of wild ginseng, powdered rhinoceros horn, licorice, scute, wood homalomena, and gardenia. Grind, decoct in water, and take after meals.[113p]

Shangqing Pills: Treats swollen and painful throat, mouth, and tongue sores, and can also refresh the spirit. Modified Peppermint Pills: Treats wind-heat throat swelling and pain. Ingredients: eight liang of peppermint leaves, one liang each of fangfeng, chuanxiong, and white cardamom, five qian each of gypsum and licorice, five fen of borneol, and two liang of jiegeng. Grind the above into a powder, mix with honey evenly, form into thirty pills from one liang, and dissolve one pill in the mouth.

Jinghuang Decoction (from "Into the Door"): Treats wind-heat stagnation, swollen and painful throat, and constipation. Ingredients: four qian of jingjie and one qian of dahuang. Chop the ingredients, boil in water, and take on an empty stomach.

Ganjiao Decoction (from "Essential Formulas"): Treats wind-heat, swollen and painful throat, or has remarkable effects on throat obstruction. Ingredients: two qian of jiegeng, one qian each of fresh licorice, jingjie spikes, fangfeng, huangqin, and peppermint. Grind these into a powder, make a decoction, and take slowly. Throat Block Recipe: Treats throat block, sore, swollen, with ulceration, unable to take water or food, and can lead to death in an instant.
Ingredients: Equal parts of Castor Seed and Asarum.
Grind into powder, roll medication in paper tightly at both ends, cut in the middle, and place into both nostrils. Immediately the head feels cool, and the throat opens up.

Throat Pain Powder: Treats throat pain, ulceration, and hoarseness.

Throat Unblock Drink: Treats throat block swelling and pain, preventing speech; all who follow this method recover.

Divine Efficacy Powder - Treats throat paralysis, causing voice loss.

Mix equal parts of Schizonepeta spikes and castor bean flesh into a powder. Form into honey-sized pills, wrap in cotton, and dissolve in the mouth.

Saliva-Removing Formula - Treats throat paralysis.

Use five qian of pig's tooth soapberry, one and a half qian of copper sulfate, five fen of indigo; grind into a powder. Mix with vinegar to form pills the size of cherries. Each pill should be wrapped in cooked silk and placed on the tip of a chopstick. Moisten with good vinegar, apply onto the throat ulcer. Bite the chopstick; if saliva flows like water, relief is achieved. Afterwards, take Fangfeng Tongsheng Powder.

Ice Plum Pills - Effective for eighteen types of throat paralysis; also treats throat wind swelling and pain remarkably.

Take thirty-five pieces of Tiannanxing, Banxia, white alum, white salt, Fangfeng, and nitrate rock (each four liang), two liang of Platycodon and one and seven-tenths liang of licorice (cooked), along with one hundred pieces of large plum fruits. Soak the nitrate in saltwater for a time, then crush all herbs, mix in water, and submerge the plum fruits in this mixture. The water level should cover the plums by three fingers. Soak for seven days, remove, and dry in the sun; then soak again, dry until the medicinal water is nearly gone. Finally, store the plums in a sealed ceramic jar; the frost-white coating is ideal. When using, wrap in cotton, hold in the mouth, and gradually swallow the juice; expectorate until recovery. An alternative recipe includes four liang of soapberry, without licorice.[117p]

Longnao Chuanxiong Pill: Treats various throat diseases, opening and benefiting the seven orifices, refreshing the spirit, clearing heat and resolving phlegm, eliminating wind and transforming stagnation. Ingredients: 5.3 taels of mint leaves, 1.5 taels of balloon flower root, 1 tael each of Chuanxiong, Fangfeng, and licorice, 0.5 taels of white cardamom, 0.3 taels of dried brain, 0.2 taels of sand ginger. Grind these ingredients into a powder, mix it with honey, and form into 20 pills for every 2 taels. Each pill should be chewed well and taken with clear tea, or dissolved in the mouth. This formula is similar to the decoction with added or subtracted mint.

Wuxiao Ointment: The throat reflects the condition of the spleen and stomach. If there is heat in the organs, the throat will become blocked, and the spirit energy will not flow freely; it is advisable to take this remedy. Ingredients: 10 taels of fresh Wuxiao, 3 taels of Cimicifuga, 2 taels each of antler horns, Tongcao, and peony root, 1 sheng of cut rose root, 5 sheng of sliced fresh Rehmannia, 2 jin of pig fat, and 6 zhu of mugwort leaves (fresh preferred). Grind these nine ingredients and wrap them in fine cloth, steep in 1 sheng of bitter wine overnight. Infuse into the pig fat over a low heat until the bitter wine evaporates and the ointment is quiet; strain out the dregs. The resulting ointment should be the size of a large almond, and should be slowly swallowed down the throat.

Another formula: For treating swollen painful throat wind and toxins impacting the heart and chest. Ingredients: 1.5 sheng of fermented soybeans, 2 taels each of rhinoceros horn, belamcanda, apricot kernels, and licorice, 3 taels of peony root, 7 pieces of gardenia, 4 taels of Cimicifuga, and 2.5 taels of antler horn. Grind these nine ingredients and decoct in 9 sheng of water until reduced to 3 sheng, then strain, add the fermented soybeans, and bring to a boil. Divide into three doses.[118p]

Wind Poison Formula: For treating wind poison when water cannot be swallowed.

Ingredients:

  • 6 taels of both Cimicifuga (Sheng Ma) and Peony (Shao Yao)
  • 3 taels each of Reed Rhizome (She Gan), Apricot Kernels (Xing Ren), Cypress gum (Feng Xiang), Kudzu Root (Ge Gen), and Ephedra (Ma Huang)
  • 2 taels of Licorice (Gan Cao)

Instructions:

  • Chew these eight ingredients and boil in eight liters of water until reduced to two and a half liters. Divide into three doses.

Mother Ginger Wine:
The throat indicates conditions of the liver and gallbladder. If there's internal heat, the throat will feel obstructed with closed breath. If there's internal cold, the throat will break and cause hoarseness. This remedy should be taken.

Ingredients:

  • 2 liters of Mother Ginger juice
  • 1 liter each of clarified butter, cow marrow, and oil
  • 1 tael each of Cinnamon (Gui Xin) and Qinjiao (Qin Jiao)
  • 1 and a half taels of Siler (Fang Feng)
  • 1 and 6/10 taels of Chuanxiong and Du Huo

Instructions:

  • Grind these nine ingredients into powder, add to ginger juice, boil gently with cow marrow and clarified butter for three cycles (up and down), then in the morning, warm 1 liter of clear wine, add 2 portions of the paste, and swallow carefully, three times a day and once at night.

Another Formula: For treating previous symptoms and throat pain with difficulty.

Ingredients:

  • 1 tael each of Danshen (Salvia), Sheng Ma, and powdered realgar (Xiong Huang)
  • 1 tael each of Apricot Kernels, Euphorbia (Gui Jiu), Licorice, and Reed Rhizome
  • Half a tael of Musk

Instructions:

  • Grind these eight ingredients into powder, make pills as big as Tongzi (a type of nut), take one pill with wine, increasing to five pills, three times a day.

Another Formula: For treating throat injury and unclear voice.

  • 1 liter each of wine and clarified butter
  • 2 and a half taels of ground dried ginger
  • 2 taels each of Tong Cao, Cinnamon, and Acorus (Shi Chang Pu)

Instructions:

  • Mix these six ingredients and take a spoonful, three times a day.[119p]

Another recipe for treating prior symptoms.
One sheng of wine and one sheng of grease, ten taels of dried ginger powder. Mix these three ingredients with two dongs of wine, one spoon of grease, and two spoons of ginger powder. Take this mixture three times a day after meals.

Another recipe for treating throat discomfort and difficulty in breathing.
One tael each of swallowwort, apricot kernel, ginseng, aconite, and cinnamon. Grind these five ingredients into a powder, form into honey pills the size of a finger, and let one dissolve slowly in the mouth to connect with the medicine.

A decoction for treating mild throat obstruction.
Two qian each of raw rehmannia, peony, ophiopogon, and salvia; one qian of licorice; and one and a half qian of achyranthes. Boil with two sheng of water until reduced by a third and take warm on an empty stomach.

An adjusted version of the decoction for cases as mentioned above but used when fire is severe.
Two qian each of raw rehmannia, peony, and ophiopogon; three to five qian of cooked rehmannia; five to seven fen of honey-fried licorice; one qian each of anemarrhena and lycium peel. Boil with two sheng of water.

A second decoction for treating throat obstruction caused by excessive thought or emotional strain leading to heart fire.
Two to three qian each of raw rehmannia and ophiopogon; two qian of jujube seed; one qian of licorice; one to two qian of coptis; and one and a half qian each of poria, cheap ginseng, and akebia. Use two sheng of water, add twenty strands of lantern grass or bamboo leaves, and boil until reduced by a third, then take on an empty stomach.[120p]

　　四阴煎　治咳嗽肺热喉痹。
　　茯苓钱半　生地二三钱　麦冬　芍药　百合　沙参各二钱　生甘草一钱　　水二锺，煎七分，食远服。

　　抽薪饮　治火证喉痹。
　　黄芩　石斛　木通　栀子炒　黄蘗各一二钱　枳壳　泽泻各钱半　细甘草三分　　水一锺半，煎七分，食远温服，甚者冷服更佳。
　　徙薪饮　治喉痹火不甚者。
　　陈皮八分　黄芩二钱　麦冬　芍药　黄蘗　茯苓　牡丹皮各一钱半　　水一锺半，煎七分，食远温服。

　　菉豆饮　治咽喉火壅诸证。
　　菉豆不拘多寡，宽汤煮糜烂，　入盐少许，或蜜亦可，待冰冷，或厚或稀或汤，任意饮食之，日或三四次不拘。此物性非寒苦，不伤脾气，且善于解毒除烦，退热止渴，大利小水，乃浅易中之最佳最捷者也。若火盛口干，不宜厚味，但略煮半熟，清汤冷饮之，尤善除烦清火。[121p]

Si Yin Decoction - Treats cough and lung heat with throat obstruction.
Poria 1.5-2 grams, raw Rehmannia 2-3 grams, Ophiopogon 2 grams, Peony 2 grams, Lily bulb 2 grams, Adenophora 2 grams, raw Licorice 1 gram. Use 500 ml of water, decoct until reduced to 350 ml, and take away from meals.

Chou Xin Drink - Treats heat symptoms with throat obstruction.
Huangqin 1-2 grams, Dendrobium 1-2 grams, Mutong 1-2 grams, stir-fried Gardenia 1-2 grams, Huangbo 1-2 grams, Zhiqiao 0.5 grams, Zexie 0.5 grams, fine Licorice 0.3 grams. Use 500 ml of water, decoct until reduced to 350 ml, and take warm away from meals; for severe cases, cold consumption is even better.

Xi Xin Drink - Treats throat obstruction with less severe heat.
Chenpi 0.8 grams, Huangqin 2 grams, Ophiopogon 1.5 grams, Peony 1.5 grams, Huangbo 1.5 grams, Poria 1.5 grams, and Moutan bark 1.5 grams. Use 500 ml of water, decoct until reduced to 350 ml, and take warm away from meals.

Lu Dou Drink - Treats various symptoms of throat heat obstruction.
Lu Dou (mung bean) in any amount, boil in ample water until mushy, add a pinch of salt or some honey, let cool; whether thick or thin, you may consume freely, up to three or four times a day as needed. This substance is not cold or bitter, does not harm spleen qi, is effective in detoxifying, alleviating annoyance, reducing heat, and quenching thirst, promoting urination, making it one of the best and easiest remedies. If there is intense heat and dry mouth, avoid rich flavors, just boil lightly, consume the clear broth cold, which is particularly effective for alleviating annoyance and clearing heat.[121p]

　　雪梨浆　治前证。

咽喉门

　　　　单方

　　缠喉风：白矾末半钱，乌鸡子清一个，调匀灌入喉中，立效如神。 【《纲目》】[122p]

Snow Pear Decoction – for treating initial symptoms.
Peel a large, fragrant, and sweet pear, and place it in a large bowl filled with cold spring water. Thinly slice the pear and soak it in the water for a short while. The water will become sweet. Drink this water frequently, but do not consume the pear pulp, as it quickly counteracts excess yin fire.

Nourishing Yin Eight-Flavor Pill – for treating yin deficiency throat pain.
Ingredients: 4 taels each of Chinese yam and cornelian cherry flesh; 3 taels each of peach kernel, poria, and herbs (salt-fried) such as anemarrhena, and berberine (salt-fried); 8 taels of cooked rehmannia. Steam and pound together, then decoct with water for oral administration.

Calming Yin Decoction – for treating heat in the throat due to excess yang. This decoction should be consumed cold.
Ingredients: 1-2 taels of cooked rehmannia, 2 qian of ox knee, 1 qian of honey-fried licorice, 1.5 qian of poria, 1-2 qian of cinnamon, 0.5-0.7 qian (or 1-2-3 qian) of processed aconite. Boil with 2 sheng of water and drink quickly.

Substitute Spoon Powder – for treating throat obstruction.
Ingredients: 1 qian each of moonstone and gypsum, 1 fen of borneol, 3 fen of powdered grass, 5 fen of fried silkworm, 5 fen of alumen, and 5 fen of candied soapwort (smoked until the smoke disappears) — finely powdered. Use a fine bamboo tube to blow this powder frequently into the throat. Adding 5 fen of ox bile is even better.

Throat Wind: Mix 0.5 qian of alum powder with one egg white of a black chicken, and inject it into the throat. It will work miraculously.[122p]

　　(石卜)硝治喉痹，神验。含口中细细咽汁，立瘥。马牙硝与焰硝同功。 【《本草》】
　　咽中疮肿：(石卜)硝一钱，蓖麻子去皮一粒，同研，新水和服，即效。【《纲目》】
　　硼砂治咽喉痹，最为要切，含化咽津。 【《本草》，下同】
　　咽喉痹痛：升麻剉煎，取汁含之。

　　喉闭垂死：取马蔺根捣绞取汁，稍稍咽之，口噤者灌下。叶及子同功。子则取四十九枚为末，水调服。叶则取二两，水煎服。
　　喉痹：取牛蒡子一合，半生半炒，为末，热酒调下一钱。　　又方：牛蒡子六分，马蔺子八分，为末，暖水调一钱服，立瘥。
　　喉痹肿痛：露蜂房灰、白僵蚕等分为末，乳香汤每服半钱。　　又方：用蜂房烧灰，每以一钱吹入喉内，不拘大人小儿。 【《心镜》】
　　喉闭，水浆不入：采射干根捣取汁，细呷之，治喉痹最捷。或酽酢同研，取汁噙，引出涎更妙。【丹溪】[123p]

(Stone nitrate) treats throat diseases effectively. Holding it in the mouth and swallowing gradually leads to healing. Ma ya nitrate has the same effect as flame nitrate.

For throat sores: one qian of (stone nitrate) and one peeled castor seed, ground together, mixed with fresh water and consumed, results in immediate effect.

Borax treats throat ailments and is particularly important; it should be dissolved in saliva.

For painful throat ailments: decoct and strain the juice of elevated hemp and hold it in the mouth.

For throat closure and imminent death: take the root of horse grass, crush and extract the juice, swallow slowly; for those who cannot open their mouths, administer via injection. Leaves and seeds have similar effects. For seeds, take forty-nine pieces, grind into powder, and mix with water to consume. For leaves, take two taels and decoct for consumption.

For throat paralysis: take one he of burdock seeds, half raw, half roasted, grind into powder and mix with hot wine to consume one qian. Another prescription: six fen of burdock seeds and eight fen of horse grass seeds, ground into powder, mixed with warm water, and consumed one qian for immediate healing.

For swollen and painful throat: mix equal parts of bee nest ash and white silkworm ash into powder, and consume half a qian with frankincense soup. Another method: use ash from burnt bee nests, blowing one qian into the throat, regardless of adult or child.

For throat closure, preventing water and food intake: extract juice from the roots of the shoot dry plant, sip it slowly; this is the quickest cure for throat paralysis. Alternatively, grind it with strong vinegar, extract the juice, and hold it in the mouth; it is even better for drawing out saliva.[123p]

　　喉痹咽肿生疮：蓖麻子取肉捶碎，纸卷作筒，烧烟吸之，治喉痹，名圣烟筒。 【《正传》】
　　马勃，治喉闭咽痛，以蜜揉拌，以水调呷。 【《本草》】　　又方：马勃、白矾等分为末，以鹅翎管吹入喉中，吐痰，妙。 【《纲目》】

　　急喉闭：皂荚捶槌碎去皮子，挼，水一盏灌下，或吐或不吐，即安。

　　喉痹、双乳蛾：壁钱窝一个，取患者脑后发，拔一根缠定钱窝，灯上以银簪挑而烧之，存性，为末，吹入患处，立消。【《回春》】　　又方：壁钱烧存性，白矾、枯发灰等分，为末，吹入喉中，治喉闭，名吹喉散。 【《医鉴》】[124p]

Throat disorders and ulceration: Take castor beans, crush the flesh, roll paper into a tube, burn and inhale the smoke to treat throat ailments, called the Sacred Smoke Tube.

For throat closure and pain in the pharynx: Use viper's bugloss mixed with honey and water to consume. Another method involves mixing viper's bugloss and alum into a powder, using a goose feather to blow it into the throat to expel phlegm, which is effective.

For throat ulcers and closure: Use good rice vinegar to gargle and spit out as needed.

For wind in the throat making it difficult to swallow: Take barley flour to make a thin porridge that is smooth and easy to swallow, aiding gastric energy.

For acute throat closure: Crush soap pods to remove the skin, then knead and drink a cup of water; whether you expel it or not, it will be beneficial.

For acute throat closure: Take a small amount of loach bile and apply it to the affected area; the illness will resolve upon application. If the condition is severe, dilute it with water. The best specimens are those collected in the twelfth lunar month.

For throat disorders and breast moths: Take a moneywort nest, use a hair from the back of the patient’s head to twist around the moneywort, burn it with a silver pin over a lamp to preserve its essence, then blow the powder into the affected area for immediate relief.

Another method: Burn moneywort to preserve its essence, mix with alum and ash from burnt hair evenly, powder it, and blow it into the throat to treat closure, known as Throat Blowing Powder.[124p]

　　喉痹：蛴螬取汁，点在喉中，即喉开。 【《本草》，下同】

Sore throat with heat: Obtain fresh pears, extract their juice, and drink frequently; taking more is beneficial.

　　喉风肿闭：用皂矾一斤，好米酢三升拌，晒干为末，吹之，痰涎出尽，用良姜末少许入茶内，漱口，咽之即愈。【《集效方》】

  • For swollen throat wind: Use one pound of soap alum, mix with three liters of good rice vinegar, dry, and grind into powder; blow it in, and phlegm will be expelled. Use a small amount of dried ginger powder in tea for gargling; swallowing it will ensure recovery.

  • For throat obstruction and pain: Grind the root of distant志 into powder and blow it; this will help expel phlegm.

  • For throat obstruction: Use aged white plums and let them ferment with silkworms; hold the plums in your mouth.

  • For hot and painful throat: Grind gentian and take it with water.

  • For swollen and painful throat: Pound the roots of horse hoof grass and mix with well water to ingest; it will be effective.

  • For swelling and pain in the throat: Use a one-inch piece of gold and hold it in the mouth to stimulate saliva.

  • For throat obstruction and swelling: Grind red mercury and swallow it with water or vinegar—it's very good.

  • In winter, for throat obstruction with back pain, where medication cannot be taken: Burn snake bed seeds in a bottle, put the mouth to the bottle and inhale slowly; phlegm will come out.

  • For heat and toxin obstructing the throat: Grind cardamom husks into powder and take one penny's worth with water.

  • For urgent throat wind: Use white fragrant flowers, grind them with water and administer.

  • For swollen and painful throat: Use tender mugwort, extract its juice, and swallow it slowly.

  • Another remedy: Take a handful of green mugwort with its stems and leaves, mix with vinegar, mash, and apply it to the throat. In winter, dried mugwort can also be used.[128p]

　　喉闭肿痛：益母草捣烂，新汲水一碗绞浓汁，顿饮随吐愈。冬月用根。 【《易简方》，下同】
　　喉痹壅塞不通：红蓝花捣绞取汁一小升服之，以瘥为度。如冬月无生花，以干者浸湿，绞汁煎服，极验。

　　喉痹肿痛：生油一合灌之，立愈。

　　饮酒咽烂，口舌生疮：大麻仁一升、黄芩二两为末，蜜丸含之。 【《千金方》】
　　咽喉肿痛，卒不可食：白面和酢涂喉外肿处。 【《普济方》】
　　喉痹痄腮：用糯米三升，于端午前四十九日，以冷水浸之，一日两换水，轻淘转，勿令搅碎，至端午日取出阴干，绢袋盛，挂通风处，每用旋取炒黑为末，冷水调如膏药，贴项下及肿处，一夜便消。干即换之，常令湿为妙。[137p]

Sore throat with obstruction and swelling, causing difficulty in breathing, leading to the risk of suffocation: Use one liang of络石草 (Liangshi grass), boil in one sheng (approximately 1 liter) of water until reduced to one large cup, and sip slowly.

For inability to speak due to throat obstruction: The root of sheep’s hoof should not be exposed to wind, sunlight, or contact with women, chickens, or dogs. Grind it in vinegar for three years until it becomes like mud, then use it to wipe the outside of the throat until it turns red, and apply it.

For throat swelling and pain, making it difficult to swallow: Take one fen of horse gall (马勃), and one section of shed snake skin, burn and grind them into a powder. Wrap one qian (approximately 3 grams) in cotton and hold it in the mouth to alleviate the symptoms immediately.

For "running horse" throat obstruction: The powder made from horse droppings and growth fungus should each be one liang. Grind them into a powder, and for each sound uttered, spitting out saliva mixed with blood will bring relief.

For sore and swollen throat: Inject with one he of fresh oil for immediate healing.

For throat rot from drinking, with sores on the tongue and mouth: Take one sheng of hemp seeds and two liang of Huangqín (Scutellaria baicalensis); grind into a powder and make honey pills to dissolve in the mouth.

For sore throat and acute inability to eat: Mix white flour with vinegar and apply it to the external swelling of the throat.

For throat obstructions in mumps: Use three sheng of glutinous rice. Soak it in cold water for forty-nine days before the Dragon Boat Festival, changing the water twice daily, gently rinsing without breaking the grains. On the day of the festival, take it out, dry it in the shade, store in a silk bag hanging in a ventilated area. Whenever needed, roast until black and grind into powder, mixing with cold water to make a plaster to apply under the jaw and on the swollen area; it will dissolve overnight. Replace when dry, keeping it moist is preferable.[137p]

　　喉痹肿痛：稻草烧取黑烟，酢调吹鼻中，或灌入喉中，滚出痰，立愈。 【《普济方》】
　　喉风肿痛：丝瓜根以瓦瓶盛水浸饮之。 【《海上名方》】
　　咽喉痹痛：五月五日收桑上木耳，白如鱼鳞者，临时捣碎，绵包弹子大，蜜汤浸，含之立效。【《便民方》】
　　喉痹乳蛾：用青梅二十枚，盐十二两，腌五日，取梅汁入明矾三两，桔梗、白芷、防风各二两，猪牙皂角三十条，俱为细末，拌汁和梅入瓶收之。每用一枚，噙咽津液，凡中风痰厥，牙关不开，用此擦之，尤佳。　　又方：梅包生矾末作丸，含咽或纳吞之。
　　喉痹塞痛：桃皮煮汁三升服。 【《千金方》】
　　咽喉作痛：茱萸末敷调涂足心，一夕愈。
　　咽喉闭痛：生乌药即矮樟根，以酸酢二盏，煎一盏，先噙后咽，吐出痰涎为愈。
　　风热喉痹：灯心一钱，黄蘗五分，并烧存性，白矾七分煅过，冰片三分，为末，每以一二分吹患处。【《集简方》】[138p]

Throat obstruction and swelling pain: Burn straw to produce black smoke, mix with vinegar and blow into the nose, or pour into the throat to expel phlegm for immediate relief.

　　卒喉痹痛：黄蘗片含之；又以一斤，酒一斗，煮二沸，恣饮便愈。 【《肘后方》】
　　咽喉卒肿，食饮不通：苦酒和黄蘗末敷之，冷即易。
　　喉风闭塞：腊月初一日，取猪胆不拘大小五六枚，用黄连、青黛、薄荷、僵蚕、白矾、(石卜)硝各五钱，装入胆内，青纸包了，将地掘一孔，方深各一尺，以竹横悬此胆在内，以物盖定，候至立春日取出，待风吹去胆皮青纸，研末密收。每吹少许，神验，乃万金不传之方。
　　大人喉风：筀竹油频饮之。 【《集简方》】
　　咽喉卒肿不下食：地龙十四条捣涂喉外；又以一条着盐化水，入蜜少许服之。
　　喉痹塞口：用韭地红小蚯蚓数条，酢擂取食之，即吐出痰血二三碗，神效。 【《普济方》】　　又方：用地龙一条，研极烂，以鸡子白搅和灌入，即通。 【《圣惠方》】
　　喉痹肿塞：用蜗牛绵裹水浸，含咽，须臾立通。　　又方：蜗牛七枚，白梅肉二枚，研烂，绵裹，含咽立效。[139p]

For sudden throat pain: Take Huangbai pills; also, mix one pound with ten dou of wine, boil twice, and drink freely until cured.

For sudden swelling of the throat that obstructs eating and drinking: Mix bitter wine with powdered Huangbai and apply to the area; it will be alleviated when cold.

For throat wind blockage: On the first day of the twelfth month, take five or six pig gallbladders of any size, use five qian each of Huanglian, Qingdai, mint, silkworm, and white alum, place them inside the gallbladder, wrap with blue paper, dig a hole a foot deep in the ground, suspend the gallbladder inside with bamboo, cover securely, and wait until the day of the spring equinox to take it out. Allow the wind to blow away the gallbladder and blue paper, then grind the remains into a fine powder and store carefully. A small amount blown out is effective, a secret formula worth its weight in gold.

For throat wind in adults: Drink bamboo oil frequently.

For sudden swelling of the throat that prevents eating: Crush fourteen earthworms and rub on the outside of the throat; also, take one worm with salt dissolved in water and a little honey to consume.

For throat blockage with difficulty in swallowing: Use several small earthworms, pound them with vinegar to eat, which will bring up two or three bowls of phlegm and blood, with remarkable effect. Another method: Use one earthworm, grind it very finely, mix with egg white, and inject, which will relieve the blockage.

For throat swelling and blockage: Use a snail soaked in water, hold it in the mouth and swallow, which will work immediately. Another method: Take seven snails, two pieces of white plum flesh, grind them together, wrap in cotton, and hold in the throat for immediate effect.[139p]

　　喉痹肿痛：鸡矢白含之咽汁。 【《圣惠方》】

　　喉痹喉风：五月五日或六月六日、七月七日，采楮桃阴干，每用一个为末，井华水服之，重者以两个即愈。【《集简方》】
　　咽喉生疮，层层如迭，不痛，日久有窍出臭气，废饮食：用臭橘叶，煎汤连服。
　　缠喉风危急：用巴豆七粒，三生四熟，生者去壳生研，熟者去壳灯上烧，存性，研；干桑黄茹二片；雄黄一块，细研；郁金一枚研。　　右再研细，每服半字，茶清少许调下。如口噤咽塞，以竹管吹入喉中，须臾吐利即安矣。名雄黄散。[140p]

Throat swelling and pain: Use lychee flowers and roots, boil them in water and sip the juice slowly, which will help in recovery. [From "Hai Shang Fang"]

A poem about throat issues: Severe throat swelling and obstruction are most concerning; quickly obtain oil from a large lamp. In serious cases, take only three or five sips; this remedy was left by a wise person.

Throat swelling and pain: Suck on chicken feces to get the juice in your throat. [From "Sheng Hui Fang"]

Throat swelling and pain: Take a piece of soapwort, peel it, soak it in rice vinegar, and roast it seven times without burning. Grind it to a powder, blow a little into the throat, and spitting saliva will result in recovery.

Throat ulcers: Layered and stacked, without pain, but after a long time, foul-smelling holes may appear, ruining appetite: use stinky tangerine leaves, boil them, and drink the decoction.
